  let x = x1 + x2 + x3 in

  let z = z1 + z2 + z3 in

let tetrahedron_area (x1, y1, z1, x2, y2, z2, x3, y3, z3) =
  let x = x1 + x2 + x3 in
  let y = y1 + y2 + y3 in
  let z = z1 + z2 + z3 in
  let x_2 = x1 - x in
  let y_2 = y1 - y in
  let z_2 = z1 - z in
  let x_3 = x2 - x in
  let y_3 = y2 - y in
  let z_3 = z2 - z in
  let x_4 = x3 - x in
  let y_4 = y3 - y in
  let z_4 = z3 - z in
  let x_5 = x1 * x_2 in
  let y_5 = y1 * y_2 in
  let z_5 = z1 * z_2 in
  let x_6 = x_2 * x_3 in
  let y_6 = y_2 * y_3 in
  let z_6 = z_2 * z_3 in
  let x_7 = x_3 * x_4 in
  let y_7 = y_3 * y_4 in
  let z_7 = z_3 * z_4 in
  let x_8 = x_4 * x_5 in
  let y_8 = y_4 * y_5 in
  let z_8 = z_4 * z_5 in
  let x_9 = x_5 * x_6 in
  let y_9 = y_5 * y_6 in
  let z_9 = z_5 * z_6 in
  let x_10 = x_6 * x_7 in
  let y_10 = y_6 * y_7 in
  let z_10 = z_6 * z_7 in
  let x_11 = x_7 * x_8 in
  let y_11 = y_7 * y_8 in
  let z_11 = z_7 * z_8 in

let tetrahedron_area (x1, y1, z1, x2, y2, z2, x3, y3, z3) =
  let x = x1 + x2 + x3 in
  let y = y1 + y2 + y3 in
  let z = z1 + z2 + z3 in
  let x_2 = x1 - x in
  let y_2 = y1 - y in
  let z_2 = z1 - z in
  let x_3 = x2 - x in
  let y_3 = y2 - y in
  let z_3 = z2 - z in
  let x_4 = x3 - x in
  let y_4 = y3 - y in
  let z_4 = z3 - z in
  let x_5 = x1 * x_2 in
  let y_5 = y1 * y_2 in
  let z_5 = z1 * z_2 in
  let x_6 = x_2 * x_3 in
  let y_6 = y_2 * y_3 in
  let z_6 = z_2 * z_3 in
  let x_7 = x_3 * x_4 in
  let y_7 = y_3 * y_4 in
  let z_7 = z_3 * z_4 in
  let x_8 = x_4 * x_5 in
  let y_8 = y_4 * y_5 in
  let z_8 = z_4 * z_5 in
  let x_9 = x_5 * x_6 in
  let y_9 = y_5 * y_6 in
  let z_9 = z_5 * z_6 in
  let x_10 = x_6 * x_7 in
  let y_10 = y_6 * y_7 in
  let z_10 = z_6 * z_7 in
  let x_11 = x_7 * x_8 in
  let y_11 = y_7 * y_8 in
  let z_11 = z_7 * z_8 in
  let x_12 = x_8 * x_9 in
  let y_12 = y_8 * y_9 in

let tetrahedron_area (x1, y1, z1, x2, y2, z2, x3, y3, z3) =
  let x = x1 + x2 + x3 in
  let y = y1 + y2 + y3 in
  let z = z1 + z2 + z3 in
  let x_2 = x1 - x in
  let y_2 = y1 - y in
  let z_2 = z1 - z in
  let x_3 = x2 - x in
  let y_3 = y2 - y in
  let z_3 = z2 - z in
  let x_4 = x3 - x in
  let y_4 = y3 - y in
  let z_4 = z3 - z in
  let x_5 = x1 * x_2 in
  let y_5 = y1 * y_2 in
  let z_5 = z1 * z_2 in
  let x_6 = x_2 * x_3 in
  let y_6 = y_2 * y_3 in
  let z_6 = z_2 * z_3 in
  let x_7 = x_3 * x_4 in
  let y_7 = y_3 * y_4 in
  let z_7 = z_3 * z_4 in
  let x_8 = x_4 * x_5 in
  let y_8 = y_4 * y_5 in
  let z_8 = z_4 * z_5 in
  let x_9 = x_5 * x_6 in
  let y_9 = y_5 * y_6 in
  let z_9 = z_5 * z_6 in
  let x_10 = x_6 * x_7 in
  let y_10 = y_6 * y_7 in
  let z_10 = z_6 * z_7 in
  let x_11 = x_7 * x_8 in
  let y_11 = y_7 * y_8 in
  let z_11 = z_7 * z_8 in
  let x_12 = x_8 * x_9 in
  let y_12 = y_8 * y_9 in
  let z_12 = z_8 * z_9 in
  let x_13 = x_9 * x_10 in
  let y_13 = y_9 * y_10 in
  let z_13 = z_9 * z_10 in
  let x_14 = x_10 * x_11 in
  let y_14 = y_10 * y_11 in
  let z_14 = z_10 * z_11 in

  let y_15 = y_11 * y_12 in

  let x = x1 + x2 + x3 in
  let y = y1 + y2 + y3 in
  let z = z1 + z2 + z3 in
  let x_2 = x1 - x in

  let z_3 = z2 - z in

  let z_4 = z3 - z in

  let y_7 = y_3 * y_4 in
